'sāmiya! niyacariyamiṇaṁ sōūṇa'mhāṇa māṇasē jāō । aigaruō saṁvēgō, tā āisa amha jaṁ kiccaṁ || 1 || 3850॥

tāṇaṁ ca rāyarāō viyarāvaḍ pavaratuṁgadhavalaharaṁ । savvaṁ pi hu sāmaggiṁ pēsittāṇaṁ bhaṇai kumaraṁ ||215 ||4106 ॥

suttō ya naravariṁdō niyavāsaharassa majjhayārammi । parivēḍhiyaṁ ca sahasā vāsaharaṁ jāmaillēhiṁ ॥ 220॥4111॥
kumarō vivaccharāō karālakaravālavāvaḍakaraggō । thakkō duvāradēsē suviṇīō pavarabhiccō vva ॥ 221॥4112॥
saṁjāyammi nisīhē nisuṇai rāyā ruyaṁtiyaṁ ramaṇiṁ । aikaruṇauccasaddēṇa nāi acaṁtaduhiya vva ॥ 222॥4113॥
taṁ nisuṇaṁtassa narāhivassa kāruṇṇarasasamaggassa । ēi na kahamavi niddā kayāvarāha vva jaha nārī ॥223॥4114॥
ābhāsiyā ya tattō naravaiṇā jāmaillayā purisā । tē vi hu kahavi pamāyā suttā nō dēti paḍisaddaṁ ॥ 224 ॥ 4115॥
tō vaccharāya kumarō jaṁpai 'āisaha dēva ! jaṁ kajjuṁ'। rāyā vi bhaṇai 'ajjuṁ kiṁ na vi vīsajjiō si tumaṁ ? ' ॥ 225 ॥ 4116॥
'āmaṁ' ti tēṇa vuttē, 'ahō ! pamāō maē kaō garuō । bīsajjiō si jaṁ navi, tā saṁpai jāhi niyaṭhāṇē ॥ 226॥4117॥

tā kuṇaha maha pasāyaṁ, āēsaṁ dēha mā cirāvēha' । raṇṇā vi hu paḍibhaṇiyaṁ 'jāhi tumaṁ, hōu ēvaṁ ' ti ॥231॥4122 ॥

annattha suṇaya- kōlhuyanivahēṇa aṇāhamaḍayasaṁghāyā । bhakkhijati jahicchaṁ kaḍayaḍarāva karēṁtēhiṁ ॥ 236॥4127॥
aṇṇattha vigayamaṁsēhiṁ vivihaparisukkanara karaṁkēhiṁ । savvattō paḍiēhiṁ jāi na parisakkiuṁ sahasā ॥ 237॥ 4128 ॥ kiṁca-

'na karēmi bhōyaṇamahaṁ jāva na vatthassa mēlaō hōi' । iya nicchyaṁ vihēuṁ dēvī pavisarai kōvaharē ॥ 274॥4165॥

tā mā māē ! khēyaṁ kuṇasu nariṁdassa ēttha atthammi | muṁcasu āgahamēyaṁ pāyavilaggāṇa amhāṇa' ॥ 280 ॥ 4171॥

dāūṇa niyayakaragahiyabīḍayaṁ tō nivō visajjēi । ēsō vi jāi niyaē gēhē jaṇaṇīṇa pāsammi ॥ 286 ॥ 4177 ||
kāūṇa pāyagahaṇaṁ karakamalaṁ dhariya uttimaṁgammi । vinnavai jahā 'vihiyaṁ ērisayaṁ tumha bhagiṇīē ॥ 287॥4178॥
tā saṁpai khamiyavvaṁ aṁvē ! jaṁ kiṁci majjha duccariyaṁ । jēṇa gavēsaṇahēuṁ vaccāmiṁ tassa vatthassa ॥288॥ 4179॥
chaṇhaṁ māsāṇaṁtē puṇō vi tuha pāyavaṁdaṇaṁ kāhaṁ । jai puṇa na ēmi kahavi hu jalaṁjalī majjha dāyavvō' ॥ 289 ॥4180॥

'āēsō ' tti bhaṇittā chakkannōvāhaṇāhi gūḍhapaō । varakhaggakhēḍayakarō niggacchai jhatti nayarīō ॥ 291॥4182॥
aṇavarayapayāṇēhiṁ baccai ēsō mahiṁ vilaṁghatō । dāhiṇadisimāsaiō jā vaccai tattha kai vi diṇē ॥ 292॥4183 ॥
bahudēsa-gāma- nagarāimaṁḍiyaṁ vasumaī nirikkhaṁtō । pattō mahāmahaṁtaṁ ēga aḍavīmuhaṁ ghōraṁ ॥293॥4184॥
pēcchai ya tahiṁ khuḍalayapaṭṭaṇaṁ tuṁgapavarapāyāraṁ । ciṁtai ya "haṁta ! kiṁ puṇa ailahuyaṁ paṭṭaṇaṁ ēyaṁ ? ॥ 294 ॥ 4185 ॥
kiṁ hōhī bhūyāṇaṁ, uyāhu jakkhāṇa rakkhasāṇaṁ vā ? | ahavā nahi nahi ēyaṁ dīsai ya cauppayaṁ jēṇa ॥ 295 ॥ 4186 ॥ 10
kiṁ vā vi vigappēhiṁ ? jaṁ hōhī taṁ tu dīsihī laggaṁ" । iya ciṁtaṁtō pattō duvāradēsammi aha tassa ॥ 296॥4187॥
pavisaṁtō ya niyacchai majjhammī tassa tuṁgapāsāyaṁ । pāsēsu lahu gihāī pavisai kōḍḍēṇa pāsā ॥ 297॥ 4188 ॥

<pb n="400 plus 92"/>

pēcchai ya tassa majjhē pavaranaraṁ varasahāē uvavituṁ । niyaparivārasamaggaṁ taṁ daṭṭhē pucchaē kaṁ ci ॥ 298 ॥ 4189 ॥
'kiṁnāmayapuramēyaṁ ? kiṁnāmō ēttha naravaī ēsa ?' । sāhēi sō vi "suṁdara ! na hōi ēyaṁ puraṁ kiṁci ॥ 299॥4190॥
kiṁtu iha nāidūrē bhūtilayaṁ nāma paṭṭaṇaṁ asthi । tattha'tthi rāyasīhō rāyā sirivairisīhō ti ॥ 300 ॥ 4191॥
tassa ya iṭṭhō sēṭṭhī asēsapuralōyanāyagō atthi । bahuriddhi bharasamiddhō supasiddhō dattaō nāma ||301 ॥ 4192 ॥
tassa ya varabhajjāē siriyādēvi tti nāmadhēyāē । jāyā pahāṇakannā pañcakkhā mayaṇaghariṇi vva ॥ 302 ॥4193॥
sā jōvvaṇammi pattā asēsarūvāiguṇagaṇasamaggā । nāmēṇaṁ siridattā jaṇaṇī - jaṇayāṇa aibhattā ॥ 303 ॥ 4194॥
tīē ya mahādōsō saṁjāō jōvvaṇammi pattāē । jō sōvai pāhariō sō marai na ēttha saṁdēhō ॥ 304 ॥ 4195॥
jai puṇa nō pāhariō sōvai tō marahiṁ satta paṇa purisā । tō raṇṇā sō bhaṇiō 'vacca tumaṁ sēṭṭhi ! aḍavīē ॥ 305 ॥4196॥
mā jaṇakhaō bhavissai nayarammiṁ tujjha dhīyadōsēṇa । niyapariyaṇaṁ gahēuṁ vaccasu, mā taṁ cirāvēhi' ॥ 306 ॥ 4197॥
ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ sō sēṭṭhī niyayapariyaṇasamaggō । mōttūṇa vasimadēsaṁ saṁpattō ēttha aḍavī ||307 ||4198॥
kāūṇa ya dhavalaharaṁ pāsōvāsēsu pariyaṇagihāī । cōrāīṇa bhaēṇa ya karēi uttuṁgapāyāraṁ ॥ 308 ॥ 4199 ॥
tā pahiya ! imō sēṭṭhī paccakkhō tujjha cēva, kiṁ bahuṇā ? । ēyaṁ ca sannivēsaṁ dattauraṁ nāma supasiddhaṁ ॥ 309॥4200॥
1. kiṁci pā0 vinā ।। 2. 'madhijāē tru0 | madhējāē pā0 । 3. 'ṇasamēyā kā0 ।। 4. ° rābēha jē0 ।।

<pb n="400 plus 93"/>

ēttha ya nivasai na'ṇṇō lōō mōttūṇa pariyaṇamimassa । kayavikkaiyajaṇō vi hu kāuṁ kayavikkayaṁ vivihaṁ ॥ 310॥4201॥
mōttūṇa paraṁ ēyaṁ rayaṇīē basai dūraō gaṁtuṁ । gōlayabaddhā ya narā vihiyā ēēṇa jē niyagā ||311 ||4202॥
1
dēi ya pabhūyadavvaṁ tēṇa ya lōbhēṇa ciṭuē savvō । ēya jaṇō para kiṁtū diṇē diṇē marai ēkkēkō ||312||4203 ॥
tā jai tumaṁ pi bīhasi, gaṁtūṇaṁ tō vasāhi aṇṇattha" । kumarō vi īsi hasiuṁ pavisai dattassa atthāṇē ॥313 ॥ 4204॥
dattō vi tayaṁ daṭṭu sasaṁbhamō āsaṇaṁ davāvēi । bhaṇai ya 'uvavisasu ihaṁ', uvavisai imō vi tō tattha ॥ 314 ॥ 4205 ॥
taṁbōlāī savvaṁ paḍivattiṁ tassa kāravēūṇa । pucchai ya āyarēṇaṁ 'vaccha ! tumaṁ āgaō kattō ? ' ॥315॥4206॥
aha vaccharāyakumarō dēi imaṁ uttaraṁ jahā 'tāya ! | ujjēṇipuravarīō kāraṇavasaō iha pattō ॥ 316 ॥ 4207॥

tāō ya kannayāō dōnni vi lāvaṇṇa-vaṇṇapuṇṇāō ।

dōnni vi varavijjāō, dōnni vi navajōvvaṇammi pattāōṁ । dōnni vi thīpavarāō, dōnni vi kīlaṁti sēcchā ॥ 419 ॥ 4310 ॥
jaṇaṇīhiṁ taō dōnni vi savvālaṁkārabhūsiyaṁgīō । piupāyabaṁdaṇatthaṁ paṭuviyāō taō tāō || 420|| 4311॥

taṁ sōuṁ naranāhō nirikkhaē maṁtiṇō muhaṁ sahasā । jaṁpai imō vi 'vayaṇaṁ na hōi tassa'nnahā dēva !' ॥507 ॥ 4398 ॥
puṇa bīyaṁ paḍihāraṁ pēsai 'jōēhi aṇṇagēhammi' । sō vi hu gavēsiūṇaṁ nivassa taṁ cēva sāhēi ||508॥ 4399॥

raṇṇā vihu saṁlattō 'kiṁ tuha bhō ! vippayāraṇāṭhāṇaṁ । amhē jēṇaṁ ēvaṁ pañcakkhaṁ vippayārēsi ? ' ॥511 ॥4402 ।।
cavai imō vi hu 'sāmiya! kaiyā haṁ aliyabhāsirō diṭṭhō ? ' । bhaṇai nivō 'tujjha gihē sāmaggī atthi nō kāvi ' ॥512॥4403 ॥

tō hiyayammi sakōvō uṭui rāyā samaggaparivārō । jā vaccai gihadārē tā pēcchai maṁḍavaṁ tuṁgaṁ ॥ 514 ॥ 4405 ॥ kērisayaṁ ? -
gayaṇaggalaggadhayavaḍamālāhiṁ niraṁtaraṁ virāyaṁtaṁ । puraō viraiyakaṁcaṇakhaṁbhuggayatōraṇavicittaṁ ॥ 515 || 4406॥

ēvaṁ uttara - paṁccuttarēhiṁ jaṁpataō khaṇadvēṇa । pattō maṁḍavadārē vimhaiō visai jōyaṁtō || 518 || 4409 || avi ya-
niyai varakhaṁbhapaṁtīu sōvaṇṇiyā, jāsu dīsaṁti maṇi-rayaṇa paṇavaṇiyā ।

jattha dīsaṁti mōttiyamayā satthiyā, jattha āsaṇahaṁ paṁtīu supasatthiyā ।

'ēgō cēva uvāō ētthaṁ vijjai aṇaṇṇastaricchō' । bhaṇai nivō 'kērisaō ?' tē vi payaṁpati 'suṇa sāmi ! ॥ 590 ॥ 4481 ।।

pasariu dhagadhagaṁtu tahiṁ khaḍḍūhiṁ, nāi kayaṁtu jaṇōhaha mahuhiṁ,
jaṁ vijjhāi na chammāsēṇa vi. taṁ jamaharu kiu maṁtijaṇēṇa vi,

puṇu vinnattu rāu 'sirisāmiya ! paṭuvi sō ēvahiṁ gayagāmiya!',
rāu vi citti visēsihiṁ tuṭuu, bīsajjai bahu dūya pahihuu,
bhāi 'nimaṁtaṇatthu jamarāyaha vaccahu sayalajīvasamabhāyaha',
jā navi kōvi jāi bīhaṁtau vaccharāu tō vuttu turaṁtau,
'jāhi vaccha ! jamarāyanimaṁtau', sō 'āēsu' bhaṇēi abhaṁtau,
jāva tēṇa ēu manniu, na vi avaganniu, tāva rāu maṇi vihasiyau,
"hū majjha paōyaṇu, nāi suōyaṇu, siddhau jaṇasupasaṁsiddha" ॥596 ॥ 4487॥
paḍivajiūṇa kumarō vi jāi jā piyayamāṇa pāsammi । tā bhaṇiō tāhiṁ imaṁ 'na ya acchasi vāriō saṁtō ॥597||4488 ॥
aipahubhattō si tumaṁ, tā ajja vi kiṁ na kuṇasi pahuvayaṇaṁ । arari pahū sō sārō paṭubai jamassa jō pāsē ।। 598 ॥ 4489 ॥
pahubhattaō si piyayama ! kuṇasi na amhārisāṇa vayaṇāiṁ । tahavi hu pariharasu imaṁ aiṭuṁ pēsaṇaṁ sāmi ! ' ॥ 599 ॥ 4490॥
tō bhaṇai imō 'suṁdari ! mā jaṁpaha ērisāī bayaṇāī । jaṁ kira maha paḍivaṇṇaṁ, palaē vi na annahā hōi' || 600॥4491॥
tō hasiya rayaṇacūlā jaṁpai 'jai ēsa nicchaō tujjha । tā jāhī tattha imō jakkhō tuha kariya paḍirūvaṁ ॥ 6201 ॥ 4492 ॥
hōsu tumaṁ pi hu guttō uvariṁ niyayassa nāha! bhavaṇassa । jēṇa vihēmō sutthaṁ savvammi vi ēttha atthammi' ||602 ॥ 4493॥
1. huṁ pā0 kā0 ॥। 2. ari kā0 ॥

tō sō kiṁkarajakkhō rūvaṁ kāūṇa vaccharāyassa । baccai nivassa pāsē visēsakayaphārasiṁgārō ||603 ॥ 4494 ॥
'sāmiya! vaccāmi ahaṁ kiṁtu maē kēttiēhiṁ divahēhiṁ । baliyavvaṁ ?' rāēṇa vi paḍibhaṇiyaṁ 'māsamēttēṇa ' ॥ 604 ॥ 4495 ॥

hā vaccharāyarahiyaṁ sunnaṁ mannēmu puravariṁ ajja । hā kaha guṇanihi ! puṇaravi vilasaṁtō ēttha dīsihisi ? ' ॥ 609 ॥ 4500 ।।
raṇṇā vi hu maṁtiyaṇō vr̥ttō 'ajjēva tāō āṇēhi' । tēṇa vi bhaṇiyaṁ 'sāmiya ! mā ēvaṁ ūsugō hōhi ॥ 610॥4501 ॥

tā jō bhaṇiō māsō tattiyamēttaṁ tu pahu ! vimālēhi' । ēvaṁ nivassa māsō vōlīṇō kahavi kicchēṇa ॥612||4503॥
vōlīṇammiya māsē pahasiyacittō nivō imaṁ bhaṇai । 'vōlīṇō naṇu māsō bhō ! aja vi kiṁ cirāvēha ? ' ॥613 ॥ 4504 ॥

saṁpēsiūṇa jakkhaṁ tattō hakkāriuṁ niyayujaṇavaṁ । kahiūṇa ya vr̥ttaṁtaṁ, āharaṇaṁ maggiō iṁdō ||6 16 ॥4507॥

gahiūṇa karē ḍaṁḍaṁ puraō saṁṭhāi vaṁtariṁdō vi । ēvaṁ ca jāi ēsō nayarīē majjhamajjhēṇaṁ ॥ 618 || 4509 ॥

taṁ sōūṇaṁ rāyā bhaṇai 'pavēsēhi' dāravālō vi । āgaṁtūṇaṁ jaṁpai 'pavisasu bhō ! taṁ aṇunnāō' ||623 ॥ 4514 ॥
jāvatthāṇē pavisai asēsasāmaṁtanayaṇamālāhiṁ । ajitō nivisai niyaṭhāṇē paṇamiya ṇarēṁdaṁ ॥ 624 ॥ 4515॥

kaha bā vi gaō ? kaha vā vi āgaō ?' kōuyaṁ vahai kiṁci । “majjhana siddhaṁ kajraṁ" iya kiṁci visāyamāvahai ॥ 626 ॥ 4517 ॥
tāṇaṁ ciya saraṇēṇa ya kiṁcī aṇurāyaraṁgamāvahai । " kaha. saṁjāyaṁ ēyaṁ ?" kiṁcī cittammi vimhaiō ॥ 627॥4518॥

'acchai sayā vi suhiō amha suhī vaccharāya ! jamarāyā ?' । bhaṇai imō vi hu 'ciṭui suhiō niccaṁ pidēva ! jamō ॥ 629॥4520 ॥

vaha ya tumhāṇuvariṁ saṇiddhabaṁdhuttaṇaṁ aṇaṇṇasamaṁ । bhaṇai ya bahukālāō tumbhēhiṁ sumariyā amhē ||630||4521॥

tumhāṇa paccayatthaṁ niyapaḍihārō ya pēsiō ēsō' । taṁ jā jōyai rāyā tā pēcchai aṇamisa'cchīyaṁ ॥ 632 ॥4523 ॥

iccēvamāi savvaṁ jā paguṇaṁ hōi tāva naranāhō । gaṇiyammi pavaralaggē patthāṇayamaṁgalē ṭhāī ॥ 659 ॥ 4550 ॥

ēvaṁ diya diya baṁda payapaṁkayaṁ muṇiṁdassa । vōlīṇammi ya māsē aṇṇattha gaō taō sūrī ||670||4561॥

sayalaṁtēuriyāṇaṁ majjhammiṁ nāyagā mahādēvī । nāmēṇa sūravēgā vijjāharavaṁsasaṁbhūyā || 7 ||4573 ॥
sō tīē samaṁ bhōē bhuṁjatō jāva acchaē tāva । aṇṇēṇa naravarēṇa uvaṇīyā kaṇṇagā pavarā || 8 || 4574 ॥

mariūṇa ēsa jāō puttō sirivīrasēṇarāyassa । āvaikālē vi daḍhaṁ saṁjujjasi vivihabhōgēhiṁ " ॥ 11 ॥। 4577 ।।

saha kaṇagavaīē । ghēttūṇa ya kaṇagavaī gaō niyanayarē । dinnaṁ ca tīē pahāṇaṁ savvasāmaggisaṁjuyaṁ uttuṁgaṁ dhavalaharaṁ ।
taō ya bīyadivasē gaō tīē bhavaṇaṁ, niviṭṭō ya dinnāsaṇē । samāḍhattō ya viṇōō paṇhuttarāīhiṁ । bhaṇiyaṁ ca
kaṇagavaīē jahā - 'nāha ! nisuṇēhi tāva paṇḍuttaramēgaṁ' । kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ - 'paḍhasu' । paḍhiyaṁ ca tīē, avi ya—
'kō viṇhuvāi saddō 1 ? kō vā vi hu sōkkhavāyagō taha ya 2 ? |
kō vā vi cayai lacchi 3 ? kō vi sigdhaṁ payaṁpēi 4 ? ॥ 9 ॥ 4909 ॥
kō vā vidukkhavāī 5 ? kō vā niṁdā vivakkhavāi 6 ? tti । bhaṇasu pahāṇaṁ ca tahā 7, sattusamūhaṁ ca taha vayasu 8 ॥10॥4910॥
kō vā vi cayai niddaṁ 9 ? majjāyāvāyagō dhaṇī kō vā 10? । kiṁ vā vi bhaṇasu satthaṁ jaṁ sattusamūhaviddavaṇaṁ ॥11॥4911॥
saṁsākharaṁti ya payaṁ kērisayaṁ vā vi vayai āyāsaṁ ? । kiṁ vā vi jōiṇō iha icchaṁti sayā ? ta taṁ tā taṁ' ॥12॥4912॥
taō kumārēṇa lahiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ— asaṁ sā raṁ' । kaṇagavaīē jaṁpiyaṁ— 'sōmi ! saṁpayaṁ tumaṁ paḍhasu' । taō
paḍhiyaṁ kumārēṇa, avi ya-
'bhaṇa lōhamabhippāyaṁ ca pāvayaṁ bhaṇasu taha ya aṁtthāṇaṁ । turayaṁ lāhaṁ ca tahā māyaṁgaṁ taha ya akkhēhi ||13|| 4913॥

daṭhṭhē nirāuhaṁ taṁ kumarō vi hu mēllaē niyaṁ khaggaṁ । abhiṭṭā tē dōnni vi payaṁḍabhuyadaṁḍajujjhēṇa ॥42॥4942 ॥

bhaṇiyaṁ ca khēttavaiṇā 'tuha māhappēṇa cēva ēyassa । jahaciṁtiyadinnaphalō siddhō savyuttamō maṁtō ॥ 46 ॥ 4946॥

ēvaṁ kaē ya bhāvaṁ vijjāhivaissa tassa jāṇissaṁ । kiṁ vā vi hu paḍivajjai' iya bhaṇiē ciṁtiuṁ suiraṁ ॥ 65 ॥ 4965॥

bōllāviyā ya cēḍī pavisaṁtī khēyarēṇa ēgēṇa । 'kiṁ bhaddē ! ussūraṁ aja kahiṁ vā vi kaṇagavaī ? ' ॥71॥ 4971॥
bhaṇiyamimīē 'na satthaṁ dēhaṁ maha ajja sāmisālīē । tēṇa ahaṁ paṭṭaviyā tumhāṇa sarūvakahaṇatthaṁ ॥ 72 ॥ 4972॥
iya sōuṁ khayaravaī jaṁpai kōvēṇa phuriyaaharōṭṭō । 'rē ! rē ! karēha ṇhavaṇaṁ tubbhē siriuṁsahasāmissa ॥ 73 ॥ 4973 ॥
ahayaṁ ca tīē dēhaṁ pāvāē karēmi suṁdaraṁ ajja' । iya sōuṁ saṁkhuddhā cēḍī sahasa tti hiyayam ॥ 74 ॥ 4974॥
kumarō vihu taṁ sōuṁ baṁdhai aha pariyaraṁ daḍhaṁ sigdhaṁ । paguṇīkarēi khaggaṁ pēcchaṇayaṁ aha priyaṁ ēttō ॥ 75 ॥ 4975 ।।
khayarāhivēṇa vi taō gahiyā kēsēsu dāsacēṁḍī sā । bhaṇiyā ya kakkasēhiṁ imēhiṁ vayaṇēhiṁ duṭṭhēhiṁ ॥ 76 ॥4976॥
